          # Paperclip allows file attachments that are stored in the filesystem. All graphical
        
      2.

          # transformations are done using the Graphics/ImageMagick command line utilities and

          #
        
      11. 
      
        
    11. 
          
          
          # Paperclip defines an attachment as any file, though it makes special considerations
        
      12. 
      
        
    12. 
          
          
          # for image files. You can declare that a model has an attached file with the
        
      13. 
      
        
    13. 
          
          
          # +has_attached_file+ method:
        
      14. 
      
        
    14. 
          
          
          #
        
      15. 
      
        
    15. 
          
          
          #   class User < ActiveRecord::Base
        
      16. 
      
        
    16. 
          
          
          #     has_attached_file :avatar, :styles => { :thumb => "100x100" }
        
      17. 
      
        
    17. 
          
          
          #   end
        
      18. 
      
        
    18. 
          
          
          #
        
      19. 
      
        
    19. 
          
          
          #   user = User.new
        
      20. 
      
        
    20. 
          
          
          #   user.avatar = params[:user][:avatar]
        
      21. 
      
        
    21. 
          
          
          #   user.avatar.url
        
      22. 
      
        
    22. 
          
          
          #   # => "/users/avatars/4/original_me.jpg"
        
      23. 
      
        
    23. 
          
          
          #   user.avatar.url(:thumb)
        
      24. 
      
        
    24. 
          
          
          #   # => "/users/avatars/4/thumb_me.jpg"
        
      25. 
      
        
    25. 
          
          
          #
        
      26. 
      
        
    26. 
          
          
          # See the +has_attached_file+ documentation for more details.
        
      27.

              # Provides configurability to Paperclip. There are a number of options available, such as:
        
      56. 
      
        
    56. 
          
          
              # * whiny: Will raise an error if Paperclip cannot process thumbnails of
        
      57. 
      
        
    57. 
          
          
              #   an uploaded image. Defaults to true.
        
      58. 
      
        
    58. 
          
          
              # * log: Logs progress to the Rails log. Uses ActiveRecord's logger, so honors
        
      59. 
      
        
    59. 
          
          
              #   log levels, etc. Defaults to true.
        
      60. 
      
        
    60. 
          
          
              # * command_path: Defines the path at which to find the command line
        
      61. 
      
        
    61. 
          
          
              #   programs if they are not visible to Rails the system's search path. Defaults to
        
      62. 
      
        
    62. 
          
          
              #   nil, which uses the first executable found in the user's search path.
        
      63. 
      
        
    63. 
          
          
              # * image_magick_path: Deprecated alias of command_path.
        
      64. 
      
        
    64. 
          1
          
              def options

                @options ||= {
        
      66. 
      
        
    66. 
          
          
                  :whiny             => true,
        
      67. 
      
        
    67. 
          
          
                  :image_magick_path => nil,
        
      68. 
      
        
    68. 
          
          
                  :command_path      => nil,
        
      69. 
      
        
    69. 
          
          
                  :log               => true,
        
      70. 
      
        
    70. 
          
          
                  :log_command       => true,
        
      71. 
      
        
    71. 
          
          
                  :swallow_stderr    => true
        
      72. 
      
        
    72. 
          
          
                }
        
      73. 
      
        
    73. 
          
          
              end

              def interpolates key, &block
        
      80.

                Paperclip::Interpolations[key] = block

              # The run method takes a command to execute and an array of parameters
        
      84. 
      
        
    84. 
          
          
              # that get passed to it. The command is prefixed with the :command_path
        
      85. 
      
        
    85. 
          
          
              # option from Paperclip.options. If you have many commands to run and
        
      86. 
      
        
    86. 
          
          
              # they are in different paths, the suggested course of action is to
        
      87. 
      
        
    87. 
          
          
              # symlink them so they are all in the same directory.
        
      88. 
      
        
    88. 
          
          
              #
        
      89. 
      
        
    89. 
          
          
              # If the command returns with a result code that is not one of the
        
      90. 
      
        
    90. 
          
          
              # expected_outcodes, a PaperclipCommandLineError will be raised. Generally
        
      91. 
      
        
    91. 
          
          
              # a code of 0 is expected, but a list of codes may be passed if necessary.
        
      92. 
      
        
    92. 
          
          
              # These codes should be passed as a hash as the last argument, like so:
        
      93. 
      
        
    93. 
          
          
              #
        
      94. 
      
        
    94. 
          
          
              #   Paperclip.run("echo", "something", :expected_outcodes => [0,1,2,3])
        
      95. 
      
        
    95. 
          
          
              #
        
      96. 
      
        
    96. 
          
          
              # This method can log the command being run when
        
      97. 
      
        
    97. 
          
          
              # Paperclip.options[:log_command] is set to true (defaults to false). This
        
      98. 
      
        
    98. 
          
          
              # will only log if logging in general is set to true as well.
        
      99. 
      
        
    99. 
          1
          
              def run cmd, *params
        
      100. 
      
        
    100. 
          
          
                if options[:image_magick_path]
        
      101. 
      
        
    101. 
          
          
                  Paperclip.log("[DEPRECATION] :image_magick_path is deprecated and will be removed. Use :command_path instead")
        
      102. 
      
        
    102. 
          
          
                end
        
      103. 
      
        
    103. 
          
          
                CommandLine.path = options[:command_path] || options[:image_magick_path]
        
      104. 
      
        
    104. 
          
          
                CommandLine.new(cmd, *params).run
        
      105. 
      
        
    105. 
          
          
              end
        
      106. 
      
        
    106.

              def processor name #:nodoc:
        
      108. 
      
        
    108. 
          
          
                name = name.to_s.camelize
        
      109. 
      
        
    109. 
          
          
                processor = Paperclip.const_get(name)
        
      110. 
      
        
    110. 
          
          
                unless processor.ancestors.include?(Paperclip::Processor)
        
      111. 
      
        
    111. 
          
          
                  raise PaperclipError.new("Processor #{name} was not found")
        
      112. 
      
        
    112. 
          
          
                end
        
      113. 
      
        
    113. 
          
          
                processor
        
      114. 
      
        
    114. 
          
          
              end
        
      115.

                end

              end

                  base.send :include, Paperclip::CallbackCompatability::Rails3

                else

                  base.send :include, Paperclip::CallbackCompatability::Rails21

      171. 
      
        
    171. 
          1
          
            module ClassMethods
        
      172. 
      
        
    172. 
          
          
              # +has_attached_file+ gives the class it is called on an attribute that maps to a file. This
        
      173. 
      
        
    173. 
          
          
              # is typically a file stored somewhere on the filesystem and has been uploaded by a user.
        
      174. 
      
        
    174. 
          
          
              # The attribute returns a Paperclip::Attachment object which handles the management of
        
      175. 
      
        
    175. 
          
          
              # that file. The intent is to make the attachment as much like a normal attribute. The
        
      176. 
      
        
    176. 
          
          
              # thumbnails will be created when the new file is assigned, but they will *not* be saved
        
      177. 
      
        
    177. 
          
          
              # until +save+ is called on the record. Likewise, if the attribute is set to +nil+ is
        
      178. 
      
        
    178. 
          
          
              # called on it, the attachment will *not* be deleted until +save+ is called. See the
        
      179. 
      
        
    179. 
          
          
              # Paperclip::Attachment documentation for more specifics. There are a number of options
        
      180. 
      
        
    180. 
          
          
              # you can set to change the behavior of a Paperclip attachment:
        
      181. 
      
        
    181. 
          
          
              # * +url+: The full URL of where the attachment is publically accessible. This can just
        
      182. 
      
        
    182. 
          
          
              #   as easily point to a directory served directly through Apache as it can to an action
        
      183. 
      
        
    183. 
          
          
              #   that can control permissions. You can specify the full domain and path, but usually
        
      184. 
      
        
    184. 
          
          
              #   just an absolute path is sufficient. The leading slash *must* be included manually for
        
      185. 
      
        
    185. 
          
          
              #   absolute paths. The default value is
        
      186. 
      
        
    186. 
          
          
              #   "/system/:attachment/:id/:style/:filename". See
        
      187. 
      
        
    187. 
          
          
              #   Paperclip::Attachment#interpolate for more information on variable interpolaton.
        
      188. 
      
        
    188. 
          
          
              #     :url => "/:class/:attachment/:id/:style_:filename"
        
      189. 
      
        
    189. 
          
          
              #     :url => "http://some.other.host/stuff/:class/:id_:extension"
        
      190. 
      
        
    190. 
          
          
              # * +default_url+: The URL that will be returned if there is no attachment assigned.
        
      191. 
      
        
    191. 
          
          
              #   This field is interpolated just as the url is. The default value is
        
      192. 
      
        
    192. 
          
          
              #   "/:attachment/:style/missing.png"
        
      193. 
      
        
    193. 
          
          
              #     has_attached_file :avatar, :default_url => "/images/default_:style_avatar.png"
        
      194. 
      
        
    194. 
          
          
              #     User.new.avatar_url(:small) # => "/images/default_small_avatar.png"
        
      195. 
      
        
    195. 
          
          
              # * +styles+: A hash of thumbnail styles and their geometries. You can find more about
        
      196. 
      
        
    196. 
          
          
              #   geometry strings at the ImageMagick website
        
      197. 
      
        
    197. 
          
          
              #   (http://www.imagemagick.org/script/command-line-options.php#resize). Paperclip
        
      198. 
      
        
    198. 
          
          
              #   also adds the "#" option (e.g. "50x50#"), which will resize the image to fit maximally
        
      199. 
      
        
    199. 
          
          
              #   inside the dimensions and then crop the rest off (weighted at the center). The
        
      200. 
      
        
    200. 
          
          
              #   default value is to generate no thumbnails.
        
      201. 
      
        
    201. 
          
          
              # * +default_style+: The thumbnail style that will be used by default URLs.
        
      202. 
      
        
    202. 
          
          
              #   Defaults to +original+.
        
      203. 
      
        
    203. 
          
          
              #     has_attached_file :avatar, :styles => { :normal => "100x100#" },
        
      204. 
      
        
    204. 
          
          
              #                       :default_style => :normal
        
      205. 
      
        
    205. 
          
          
              #     user.avatar.url # => "/avatars/23/normal_me.png"
        
      206. 
      
        
    206. 
          
          
              # * +whiny+: Will raise an error if Paperclip cannot post_process an uploaded file due
        
      207. 
      
        
    207. 
          
          
              #   to a command line error. This will override the global setting for this attachment.
        
      208. 
      
        
    208. 
          
          
              #   Defaults to true. This option used to be called :whiny_thumbanils, but this is
        
      209. 
      
        
    209. 
          
          
              #   deprecated.
        
      210. 
      
        
    210. 
          
          
              # * +convert_options+: When creating thumbnails, use this free-form options
        
      211. 
      
        
    211. 
          
          
              #   array to pass in various convert command options.  Typical options are "-strip" to
        
      212. 
      
        
    212. 
          
          
              #   remove all Exif data from the image (save space for thumbnails and avatars) or
        
      213. 
      
        
    213. 
          
          
              #   "-depth 8" to specify the bit depth of the resulting conversion.  See ImageMagick
        
      214. 
      
        
    214. 
          
          
              #   convert documentation for more options: (http://www.imagemagick.org/script/convert.php)
        
      215. 
      
        
    215. 
          
          
              #   Note that this option takes a hash of options, each of which correspond to the style
        
      216. 
      
        
    216. 
          
          
              #   of thumbnail being generated. You can also specify :all as a key, which will apply
        
      217. 
      
        
    217. 
          
          
              #   to all of the thumbnails being generated. If you specify options for the :original,
        
      218. 
      
        
    218. 
          
          
              #   it would be best if you did not specify destructive options, as the intent of keeping
        
      219. 
      
        
    219. 
          
          
              #   the original around is to regenerate all the thumbnails when requirements change.
        
      220. 
      
        
    220. 
          
          
              #     has_attached_file :avatar, :styles => { :large => "300x300", :negative => "100x100" }
        
      221. 
      
        
    221. 
          
          
              #                                :convert_options => {
        
      222. 
      
        
    222. 
          
          
              #                                  :all => "-strip",
        
      223. 
      
        
    223. 
          
          
              #                                  :negative => "-negate"
        
      224. 
      
        
    224. 
          
          
              #                                }
        
      225. 
      
        
    225. 
          
          
              #   NOTE: While not deprecated yet, it is not recommended to specify options this way.
        
      226. 
      
        
    226. 
          
          
              #   It is recommended that :convert_options option be included in the hash passed to each
        
      227. 
      
        
    227. 
          
          
              #   :styles for compatability with future versions.
        
      228. 
      
        
    228. 
          
          
              #   NOTE: Strings supplied to :convert_options are split on space in order to undergo
        
      229. 
      
        
    229. 
          
          
              #   shell quoting for safety. If your options require a space, please pre-split them
        
      230. 
      
        
    230. 
          
          
              #   and pass an array to :convert_options instead.
        
      231. 
      
        
    231. 
          
          
              # * +storage+: Chooses the storage backend where the files will be stored. The current
        
      232. 
      
        
    232. 
          
          
              #   choices are :filesystem and :s3. The default is :filesystem. Make sure you read the
        
      233. 
      
        
    233. 
          
          
              #   documentation for Paperclip::Storage::Filesystem and Paperclip::Storage::S3
        
      234. 
      
        
    234. 
          
          
              #   for backend-specific options.
        
      235. 
      
        
    235. 
          1
          
              def has_attached_file name, options = {}
        
      236. 
      
        
    236. 
          2
          
                include InstanceMethods
        
      237. 
      
        
    237. 
          
          
          
        
      238. 
      
        
    238. 
          2
          
                write_inheritable_attribute(:attachment_definitions, {}) if attachment_definitions.nil?
        
      239. 
      
        
    239. 
          2
          
                attachment_definitions[name] = {:validations => []}.merge(options)
        
      240. 
      
        
    240. 
          
          
          
        
      241. 
      
        
    241. 
          2
          
                after_save :save_attached_files
        
      242. 
      
        
    242. 
          2
          
                before_destroy :destroy_attached_files
        
      243. 
      
        
    243. 
          
          
          
        
      244. 
      
        
    244. 
          2
          
                define_paperclip_callbacks :post_process, :"#{name}_post_process"
        
      245. 
      
        
    245. 
          
          
          
        
      246. 
      
        
    246. 
          2
          
                define_method name do |*args|
        
      247. 
      
        
    247. 
          
          
                  a = attachment_for(name)
        
      248. 
      
        
    248. 
          
          
                  (args.length > 0) ? a.to_s(args.first) : a

    20.

    21. 
          
          
              # WillPaginate adds +paginate+, +per_page+ and other methods to
        
      22.

    33.

      34. 
      
        
    34.

      35. 
      
        
    35.

    41. 
          
          
              #
        
      42. 
      
        
    42. 
          
          
              # In ActiveRecord finders, <tt>:order</tt> parameter specifies columns for
        
      43. 
      
        
    43. 
          
          
              # the <tt>ORDER BY</tt> clause in SQL. It is important to have it, since
        
      44. 
      
        
    44.

      45. 
      
        
    45. 
          
          
              # BY</tt> clause, databases aren't required to do consistent ordering when
        
      46. 
      
        
    46.

      47. 
      
        
    47.

      48. 
      
        
    48. 
          
          
              #

                def paginate_by_sql(sql, options)
        
      129. 
      
        
    129. 
          
          
                  WillPaginate::Collection.create(*wp_parse_options(options)) do |pager|

                def wp_count(options, args, finder)
        
      183. 
      
        
    183. 
          
          
                  excludees = [:count, :order, :limit, :offset, :readonly]
        
      184. 
      
        
    184.

      185. 
      
        
    185.

      186. 
      
        
    186.

      187. 
      
        
    187. 
          
          
          
        
      188. 
      
        
    188. 
          
          
                  # count expects (almost) the same options as find
        
      189. 
      
        
    189. 
          
          
                  count_options = options.except *excludees
        
      190. 
      
        
    190. 
          
          
          
        
      191. 
      
        
    191. 
          
          
                  # merge the hash found in :count
        
      192. 
      
        
    192. 
          
          
                  # this allows you to specify :select, :order, or anything else just for the count query
        
      193. 
      
        
    193. 
          
          
                  count_options.update options[:count] if options[:count]
        
      194. 
      
        
    194. 
          
          
                  
        
      195. 
      
        
    195. 
          
          
                  # we may be in a model or an association proxy
        
      196. 
      
        
    196. 
          
          
                  klass = (@owner and @reflection) ? @reflection.klass : self
        
      197. 
      
        
    197. 
          
          
                  
        
      198. 
      
        
    198. 
          
          
                  # forget about includes if they are irrelevant (Rails 2.1)
        
      199. 
      
        
    199. 
          
          
                  if count_options[:include] and
        
      200. 
      
        
    200. 
          
          
                      klass.private_methods.include?('references_eager_loaded_tables?') and
        
      201. 
      
        
    201. 
          
          
                      !klass.send(:references_eager_loaded_tables?, count_options)
        
      202. 
      
        
    202. 
          
          
                    count_options.delete :include
        
      203. 
      
        
    203. 
          
          
                  end
        
      204. 
      
        
    204. 
          
          
          
        
      205. 
      
        
    205. 
          
          
                  # we may have to scope ...
        
      206. 
      
        
    206. 
          
          
                  counter = Proc.new { count(count_options) }
        
      207. 
      
        
    207. 
          
          
          
        
      208. 
      
        
    208. 
          
          
                  count = if finder.index('find_') == 0 and klass.respond_to?(scoper = finder.sub('find', 'with'))
        
      209. 
      
        
    209. 
          
          
                            # scope_out adds a 'with_finder' method which acts like with_scope, if it's present
        
      210. 
      
        
    210.

      211. 
      
        
    211.

      212. 
      
        
    212.

      213. 
      
        
    213. 
          
          
                            # extract conditions from calls like "paginate_by_foo_and_bar"
        
      214. 
      
        
    214. 
          
          
                            attribute_names = extract_attribute_names_from_match(match)
        
      215. 
      
        
    215. 
          
          
                            conditions = construct_attributes_from_arguments(attribute_names, args)
        
      216. 
      
        
    216. 
          
          
                            with_scope(:find => { :conditions => conditions }, &counter)
        
      217. 
      
        
    217. 
          
          
                          else
        
      218. 
      
        
    218. 
          
          
                            counter.call
        
      219. 
      
        
    219. 
          
          
                          end
        
      220. 
      
        
    220. 
          
          
          
        
      221. 
      
        
    221. 
          
          
                  count.respond_to?(:length) ? count.length : count
        
      222. 
      
        
    222. 
          
          
                end

                def wp_parse_options(options) #:nodoc:
        
      225. 
      
        
    225. 
          
          
                  raise ArgumentError, 'parameter hash expected' unless options.respond_to? :symbolize_keys
        
      226. 
      
        
    226. 
          
          
                  options = options.symbolize_keys
        
      227. 
      
        
    227. 
          
          
                  raise ArgumentError, ':page parameter required' unless options.key? :page
        
      228. 
      
        
    228. 
          
          
                  
        
      229. 
      
        
    229. 
          
          
                  if options[:count] and options[:total_entries]
        
      230. 
      
        
    230. 
          
          
                    raise ArgumentError, ':count and :total_entries are mutually exclusive'
        
      231. 
      
        
    231. 
          
          
                  end
        
      232. 
      
        
    232. 
          
          
          
        
      233. 
      
        
    233. 
          
          
                  page     = options[:page] || 1
        
      234. 
      
        
    234. 
          
          
                  per_page = options[:per_page] || self.per_page
        
      235. 
      
        
    235. 
          
          
                  total    = options[:total_entries]
        
      236. 
      
        
    236. 
          
          
                  [page, per_page, total]
        
      237. 
      
        
    237. 
          
          
                end

      15.

            # override default options on the global level:
        
      16. 
      
        
    16. 
          
          
            #
        
      17.

    18.

              # Renders Digg/Flickr-style pagination for a WillPaginate::Collection
        
      39. 
      
        
    39. 
          
          
              # object. Nil is returned if there is only one page in total; no point in

              # * <tt>:params</tt> -- additional parameters when generating pagination links

      52.

              # * <tt>:container</tt> -- toggles rendering of the DIV container for pagination links, set to
        
      56. 
      
        
    56. 
          
          
              #   false only when you are rendering your own pagination markup (default: true)
        
      57. 
      
        
    57. 
          
          
              # * <tt>:id</tt> -- HTML ID for the container (default: nil). Pass +true+ to have the ID
        
      58. 
      
        
    58. 
          
          
              #   automatically generated from the class name of objects in collection: for example, paginating
        
      59.

      60.

                return nil unless WillPaginate::ViewHelpers.total_pages_for_collection(collection) > 1
        
      93. 
      
        
    93. 
          
          
                
        
      94. 
      
        
    94. 
          
          
                options = options.symbolize_keys.reverse_merge WillPaginate::ViewHelpers.pagination_options
        
      95. 
      
        
    95. 
          
          
                
        
      96. 
      
        
    96. 
          
          
                # get the renderer instance
        
      97. 
      
        
    97. 
          
          
                renderer = case options[:renderer]
        
      98. 
      
        
    98. 
          
          
                when String
        
      99. 
      
        
    99. 
          
          
                  options[:renderer].to_s.constantize.new
        
      100. 
      
        
    100. 
          
          
                when Class
        
      101. 
      
        
    101. 
          
          
                  options[:renderer].new
        
      102. 
      
        
    102. 
          
          
                else
        
      103. 
      
        
    103. 
          
          
                  options[:renderer]
        
      104. 
      
        
    104. 
          
          
                end
        
      105. 
      
        
    105. 
          
          
                # render HTML for pagination
        
      106. 
      
        
    106. 
          
          
                renderer.prepare collection, options, self
        
      107. 
      
        
    107. 
          
          
                renderer.to_html
        
      108. 
      
        
    108. 
          
          
              end
        
      109. 
      
        
    109. 
          
          
              
        
      110. 
      
        
    110. 
          
          
              # Wrapper for rendering pagination links at both top and bottom of a block
        
      111. 
      
        
    111. 
          
          
              # of content.
        
      112. 
      
        
    112. 
          
          
              # 
        
      113. 
      
        
    113. 
          
          
              #   <% paginated_section @posts do %>
        
      114. 
      
        
    114. 
          
          
              #     <ol id="posts">
        
      115. 
      
        
    115. 
          
          
              #       <% for post in @posts %>
        
      116. 
      
        
    116. 
          
          
              #         <li> ... </li>
        
      117. 
      
        
    117. 
          
          
              #       <% end %>
        
      118. 
      
        
    118. 
          
          
              #     </ol>
        
      119. 
      
        
    119. 
          
          
              #   <% end %>
        
      120. 
      
        
    120. 
          
          
              #
        
      121. 
      
        
    121. 
          
          
              # will result in:
        
      122. 
      
        
    122. 
          
          
              #
        
      123. 
      
        
    123. 
          
          
              #   <div class="pagination"> ... </div>
        
      124. 
      
        
    124. 
          
          
              #   <ol id="posts">
        
      125. 
      
        
    125. 
          
          
              #     ...
        
      126. 
      
        
    126. 
          
          
              #   </ol>
        
      127. 
      
        
    127. 
          
          
              #   <div class="pagination"> ... </div>
        
      128. 
      
        
    128. 
          
          
              #
        
      129. 
      
        
    129. 
          
          
              # Arguments are passed to a <tt>will_paginate</tt> call, so the same options
        
      130. 
      
        
    130. 
          
          
              # apply. Don't use the <tt>:id</tt> option; otherwise you'll finish with two
        
      131. 
      
        
    131. 
          
          
              # blocks of pagination links sharing the same ID (which is invalid HTML).
        
      132. 
      
        
    132. 
          1
          
              def paginated_section(*args, &block)
        
      133. 
      
        
    133. 
          
          
                pagination = will_paginate(*args).to_s
        
      134. 
      
        
    134. 
          
          
                content = pagination + capture(&block) + pagination
        
      135. 
      
        
    135. 
          
          
                concat content, block.binding
        
      136. 
      
        
    136. 
          
          
              end
        
      137. 
      
        
    137. 
          
          
          
        
      138. 
      
        
    138. 
          
          
              # Renders a helpful message with numbers of displayed vs. total entries.
        
      139. 
      
        
    139. 
          
          
              # You can use this as a blueprint for your own, similar helpers.
        
      140. 
      
        
    140. 
          
          
              #
        
      141. 
      
        
    141. 
          
          
              #   <%= page_entries_info @posts %>
        
      142. 
      
        
    142. 
          
          
              #   #-> Displaying posts 6 - 10 of 26 in total
        
      143. 
      
        
    143. 
          
          
              #
        
      144. 
      
        
    144. 
          
          
              # By default, the message will use the humanized class name of objects
        
      145. 
      
        
    145. 
          
          
              # in collection: for instance, "project types" for ProjectType models.
        
      146. 
      
        
    146. 
          
          
              # Override this to your liking with the <tt>:entry_name</tt> parameter:
        
      147. 
      
        
    147. 
          
          
              #
        
      148. 
      
        
    148. 
          
          
              #   <%= page_entries_info @posts, :entry_name => 'item' %>
        
      149. 
      
        
    149. 
          
          
              #   #-> Displaying items 6 - 10 of 26 in total
        
      150. 
      
        
    150. 
          1
          
              def page_entries_info(collection, options = {})
        
      151. 
      
        
    151. 
          
          
                entry_name = options[:entry_name] ||
        
      152. 
      
        
    152. 
          
          
                  (collection.empty?? 'entry' : collection.first.class.name.underscore.sub('_', ' '))
        
      153. 
      
        
    153. 
          
          
                
        
      154. 
      
        
    154. 
          
          
                if collection.total_pages < 2
        
      155. 
      
        
    155. 
          
          
                  case collection.size
        
      156. 
      
        
    156. 
          
          
                  when 0; "No #{entry_name.pluralize} found"
        
      157. 
      
        
    157. 
          
          
                  when 1; "Displaying <b>1</b> #{entry_name}"
        
      158. 
      
        
    158. 
          
          
                  else;   "Displaying <b>all #{collection.size}</b> #{entry_name.pluralize}"
        
      159. 
      
        
    159. 
          
          
                  end
        
      160. 
      
        
    160. 
          
          
                else
        
      161. 
      
        
    161. 
          
          
                  %{Displaying #{entry_name.pluralize} <b>%d&nbsp;-&nbsp;%d</b> of <b>%d</b> in total} % [
        
      162. 
      
        
    162. 
          
          
                    collection.offset + 1,
        
      163. 
      
        
    163. 
          
          
                    collection.offset + collection.length,
        
      164. 
      
        
    164. 
          
          
                    collection.total_entries
        
      165. 
      
        
    165. 
          
          
                  ]
        
      166. 
      
        
    166. 
          
          
                end
        
      167. 
      
        
    167. 
          
          
              end
        
      168. 
      
        
    168. 
          
          
          
        
      169. 
      
        
    169. 
          1
          
              def self.total_pages_for_collection(collection) #:nodoc:
        
      170. 
      
        
    170. 
          
          
                if collection.respond_to?('page_count') and !collection.respond_to?('total_pages')
        
      171. 
      
        
    171. 
          
          
                  WillPaginate::Deprecation.warn <<-MSG
        
      172. 
      
        
    172. 
          
          
                    You are using a paginated collection of class #{collection.class.name}
        
      173. 
      
        
    173. 
          
          
                    which conforms to the old API of WillPaginate::Collection by using
        
      174. 
      
        
    174. 
          
          
                    `page_count`, while the current method name is `total_pages`. Please
        
      175. 
      
        
    175. 
          
          
                    upgrade yours or 3rd-party code that provides the paginated collection.
        
      176. 
      
        
    176. 
          
          
                  MSG
        
      177. 
      
        
    177. 
          
          
                  class << collection
        
      178. 
      
        
    178. 
          
          
                    def total_pages; page_count; end
        
      179. 
      
        
    179. 
          
          
                  end
        
      180. 
      
        
    180. 
          
          
                end
        
      181. 
      
        
    181. 
          
          
                collection.total_pages
        
      182. 
      
        
    182. 
          
          
              end
        
      183. 
      
        
    183. 
          
          
            end
        
      184. 
      
        
    184. 
          
          
          
        
      185. 
      
        
    185. 
          
          
            # This class does the heavy lifting of actually building the pagination
        
      186. 
      
        
    186. 
          
          
            # links. It is used by +will_paginate+ helper internally.
        
      187. 
      
        
    187. 
          1
          
            class LinkRenderer
        
      188. 
      
        
    188. 
          
          
          
        
      189. 
      
        
    189. 
          
          
              # The gap in page links is represented by:
        
      190. 
      
        
    190. 
          
          
              #
        
      191. 
      
        
    191. 
          
          
              #   <span class="gap">&hellip;</span>
        
      192. 
      
        
    192. 
          1
          
              attr_accessor :gap_marker
        
      193. 
      
        
    193. 
          
          
              
        
      194. 
      
        
    194. 
          1
          
              def initialize
        
      195. 
      
        
    195. 
          
          
                @gap_marker = '<span class="gap">&hellip;</span>'
        
      196. 
      
        
    196. 
          
          
              end
        
      197. 
      
        
    197. 
          
          
              
        
      198. 
      
        
    198. 
          
          
              # * +collection+ is a WillPaginate::Collection instance or any other object
        
      199. 
      
        
    199. 
          
          
              #   that conforms to that API
        
      200. 
      
        
    200. 
          
          
              # * +options+ are forwarded from +will_paginate+ view helper
        
      201. 
      
        
    201. 
          
          
              # * +template+ is the reference to the template being rendered
        
      202. 
      
        
    202. 
          1
          
              def prepare(collection, options, template)
        
      203. 
      
        
    203. 
          
          
                @collection = collection
        
      204. 
      
        
    204. 
          
          
                @options    = options
        
      205. 
      
        
    205. 
          
          
                @template   = template
        
      206. 
      
        
    206. 
          
          
          
        
      207. 
      
        
    207. 
          
          
                # reset values in case we're re-using this instance
        
      208. 
      
        
    208. 
          
          
                @total_pages = @param_name = @url_string = nil
        
      209. 
      
        
    209. 
          
          
              end
        
      210. 
      
        
    210. 
          
          
          
        
      211. 
      
        
    211. 
          
          
              # Process it! This method returns the complete HTML string which contains
        
      212. 
      
        
    212. 
          
          
              # pagination links. Feel free to subclass LinkRenderer and change this
        
      213. 
      
        
    213. 
          
          
              # method as you see fit.
        
      214. 
      
        
    214. 
          1
          
              def to_html
        
      215. 
      
        
    215. 
          
          
                links = @options[:page_links] ? windowed_links : []
        
      216. 
      
        
    216. 
          
          
                # previous/next buttons
        
      217. 
      
        
    217. 
          
          
                links.unshift page_link_or_span(@collection.previous_page, 'disabled prev_page', @options[:prev_label])
        
      218. 
      
        
    218. 
          
          
                links.push    page_link_or_span(@collection.next_page,     'disabled next_page', @options[:next_label])
        
      219. 
      
        
    219. 
          
          
                
        
      220. 
      
        
    220. 
          
          
                html = links.join(@options[:separator])
        
      221. 
      
        
    221. 
          
          
                @options[:container] ? @template.content_tag(:div, html, html_attributes) : html
        
      222. 
      
        
    222. 
          
          
              end
        
      223. 
      
        
    223. 
          
          
          
        
      224. 
      
        
    224. 
          
          
              # Returns the subset of +options+ this instance was initialized with that
        
      225. 
      
        
    225. 
          
          
              # represent HTML attributes for the container element of pagination links.
        
      226. 
      
        
    226. 
          1
          
              def html_attributes
        
      227. 
      
        
    227. 
          
          
                return @html_attributes if @html_attributes
        
      228. 
      
        
    228. 
          
          
                @html_attributes = @options.except *(WillPaginate::ViewHelpers.pagination_options.keys - [:class])
        
      229. 
      
        
    229. 
          
          
                # pagination of Post models will have the ID of "posts_pagination"
        
      230. 
      
        
    230. 
          
          
                if @options[:container] and @options[:id] === true
        
      231. 
      
        
    231. 
          
          
                  @html_attributes[:id] = @collection.first.class.name.underscore.pluralize + '_pagination'
        
      232. 
      
        
    232. 
          
          
                end
        
      233. 
      
        
    233. 
          
          
                @html_attributes
        
      234. 
      
        
    234. 
          
          
              end
        
      235. 
      
        
    235. 
          
          
              
        
      236. 
      
        
    236. 
          1
          
            protected
        
      237. 
      
        
    237. 
          
          
          
        
      238. 
      
        
    238. 
          
          
              # Collects link items for visible page numbers.
        
      239. 
      
        
    239. 
          1
          
              def windowed_links
        
      240. 
      
        
    240. 
          
          
                prev = nil
        
      241. 
      
        
    241. 
          
          
          
        
      242. 
      
        
    242. 
          
          
                visible_page_numbers.inject [] do |links, n|
        
      243. 
      
        
    243. 
          
          
                  # detect gaps:
        
      244. 
      
        
    244. 
          
          
                  links << gap_marker if prev and n > prev + 1
        
      245. 
      
        
    245. 
          
          
                  links << page_link_or_span(n, 'current')
        
      246. 
      
        
    246. 
          
          
                  prev = n
        
      247. 
      
        
    247. 
          
          
                  links
        
      248. 
      
        
    248. 
          
          
                end
        
      249. 
      
        
    249. 
          
          
              end
        
      250. 
      
        
    250. 
          
          
          
        
      251. 
      
        
    251. 
          
          
              # Calculates visible page numbers using the <tt>:inner_window</tt> and
        
      252. 
      
        
    252. 
          
          
              # <tt>:outer_window</tt> options.
        
      253. 
      
        
    253. 
          1
          
              def visible_page_numbers
        
      254. 
      
        
    254. 
          
          
                inner_window, outer_window = @options[:inner_window].to_i, @options[:outer_window].to_i
        
      255. 
      
        
    255. 
          
          
                window_from = current_page - inner_window
        
      256. 
      
        
    256. 
          
          
                window_to = current_page + inner_window
        
      257. 
      
        
    257. 
          
          
                
        
      258. 
      
        
    258. 
          
          
                # adjust lower or upper limit if other is out of bounds
        
      259. 
      
        
    259. 
          
          
                if window_to > total_pages
        
      260. 
      
        
    260. 
          
          
                  window_from -= window_to - total_pages
        
      261. 
      
        
    261. 
          
          
                  window_to = total_pages
        
      262. 
      
        
    262. 
          
          
                end
        
      263. 
      
        
    263. 
          
          
                if window_from < 1
        
      264. 
      
        
    264. 
          
          
                  window_to += 1 - window_from
        
      265. 
      
        
    265. 
          
          
                  window_from = 1
        
      266. 
      
        
    266. 
          
          
                  window_to = total_pages if window_to > total_pages
        
      267. 
      
        
    267. 
          
          
                end
        
      268. 
      
        
    268. 
          
          
                
        
      269. 
      
        
    269. 
          
          
                visible   = (1..total_pages).to_a
        
      270. 
      
        
    270. 
          
          
                left_gap  = (2 + outer_window)...window_from
        
      271. 
      
        
    271. 
          
          
                right_gap = (window_to + 1)...(total_pages - outer_window)
        
      272. 
      
        
    272. 
          
          
                visible  -= left_gap.to_a  if left_gap.last - left_gap.first > 1
        
      273. 
      
        
    273. 
          
          
                visible  -= right_gap.to_a if right_gap.last - right_gap.first > 1
        
      274. 
      
        
    274. 
          
          
          
        
      275. 
      
        
    275. 
          
          
                visible
        
      276. 
      
        
    276. 
          
          
              end
        
      277. 
      
        
    277. 
          
          
              
        
      278. 
      
        
    278. 
          1
          
              def page_link_or_span(page, span_class, text = nil)
        
      279. 
      
        
    279. 
          
          
                text ||= page.to_s
        
      280. 
      
        
    280. 
          
          
                
        
      281. 
      
        
    281. 
          
          
                if page and page != current_page
        
      282. 
      
        
    282. 
          
          
                  classnames = span_class && span_class.index(' ') && span_class.split(' ', 2).last
        
      283. 
      
        
    283. 
          
          
                  page_link page, text, :rel => rel_value(page), :class => classnames
        
      284. 
      
        
    284. 
          
          
                else
        
      285. 
      
        
    285. 
          
          
                  page_span page, text, :class => span_class
        
      286. 
      
        
    286. 
          
          
                end
        
      287. 
      
        
    287. 
          
          
              end
        
      288. 
      
        
    288. 
          
          
          
        
      289. 
      
        
    289. 
          1
          
              def page_link(page, text, attributes = {})
        
      290. 
      
        
    290. 
          
          
                @template.link_to text, url_for(page), attributes
        
      291. 
      
        
    291. 
          
          
              end
        
      292. 
      
        
    292. 
          
          
          
        
      293. 
      
        
    293. 
          1
          
              def page_span(page, text, attributes = {})
        
      294. 
      
        
    294. 
          
          
                @template.content_tag :span, text, attributes
        
      295. 
      
        
    295. 
          
          
              end
        
      296. 
      
        
    296. 
          
          
          
        
      297. 
      
        
    297. 
          
          
              # Returns URL params for +page_link_or_span+, taking the current GET params
        
      298. 
      
        
    298. 
          
          
              # and <tt>:params</tt> option into account.
        
      299. 
      
        
    299. 
          1
          
              def url_for(page)
        
      300. 
      
        
    300. 
          
          
                page_one = page == 1
        
      301. 
      
        
    301. 
          
          
                unless @url_string and !page_one
        
      302. 
      
        
    302. 
          
          
                  @url_params = {}
        
      303. 
      
        
    303. 
          
          
                  # page links should preserve GET parameters
        
      304. 
      
        
    304. 
          
          
                  stringified_merge @url_params, @template.params if @template.request.get?
        
      305. 
      
        
    305. 
          
          
                  stringified_merge @url_params, @options[:params] if @options[:params]
        
      306. 
      
        
    306. 
          
          
                  
        
      307. 
      
        
    307. 
          
          
                  if complex = param_name.index(/[^\w-]/)
        
      308. 
      
        
    308. 
          
          
                    page_param = (defined?(CGIMethods) ? CGIMethods : ActionController::AbstractRequest).
        
      309. 
      
        
    309. 
          
          
                      parse_query_parameters("#{param_name}=#{page}")
        
      310. 
      
        
    310. 
          
          
                    
        
      311. 
      
        
    311. 
          
          
                    stringified_merge @url_params, page_param
        
      312. 
      
        
    312. 
          
          
                  else
        
      313. 
      
        
    313. 
          
          
                    @url_params[param_name] = page_one ? 1 : 2
        
      314. 
      
        
    314. 
          
          
                  end
        
      315. 
      
        
    315. 
          
          
          
        
      316. 
      
        
    316. 
          
          
                  url = @template.url_for(@url_params)
        
      317. 
      
        
    317. 
          
          
                  return url if page_one
        
      318. 
      
        
    318. 
          
          
                  
        
      319. 
      
        
    319. 
          
          
                  if complex
        
      320. 
      
        
    320. 
          
          
                    @url_string = url.sub(%r!((?:\?|&amp;)#{CGI.escape param_name}=)#{page}!, '\1@')
        
      321. 
      
        
    321. 
          
          
                    return url
        
      322. 
      
        
    322. 
          
          
                  else
        
      323. 
      
        
    323. 
          
          
                    @url_string = url
        
      324. 
      
        
    324. 
          
          
                    @url_params[param_name] = 3
        
      325. 
      
        
    325. 
          
          
                    @template.url_for(@url_params).split(//).each_with_index do |char, i|
        
      326. 
      
        
    326. 
          
          
                      if char == '3' and url[i, 1] == '2'
        
      327. 
      
        
    327. 
          
          
                        @url_string[i] = '@'
        
      328. 
      
        
    328. 
          
          
                        break
        
      329. 
      
        
    329. 
          
          
                      end
        
      330. 
      
        
    330. 
          
          
                    end
        
      331. 
      
        
    331. 
          
          
                  end
        
      332. 
      
        
    332. 
          
          
                end
        
      333. 
      
        
    333. 
          
          
                # finally!
        
      334. 
      
        
    334. 
          
          
                @url_string.sub '@', page.to_s
        
      335. 
      
        
    335. 
          
          
              end
        
      336. 
      
        
    336. 
          
          
          
        
      337. 
      
        
    337. 
          1
          
            private
        
      338. 
      
        
    338. 
          
          
          
        
      339. 
      
        
    339. 
          1
          
              def rel_value(page)
        
      340. 
      
        
    340. 
          
          
                case page
        
      341. 
      
        
    341. 
          
          
                when @collection.previous_page; 'prev' + (page == 1 ? ' start' : '')
        
      342. 
      
        
    342. 
          
          
                when @collection.next_page; 'next'
        
      343. 
      
        
    343. 
          
          
                when 1; 'start'
        
      344. 
      
        
    344. 
          
          
                end
        
      345. 
      
        
    345. 
          
          
              end
        
      346. 
      
        
    346. 
          
          
          
        
      347. 
      
        
    347. 
          1
          
              def current_page
        
      348. 
      
        
    348. 
          
          
                @collection.current_page
        
      349. 
      
        
    349. 
          
          
              end
        
      350. 
      
        
    350. 
          
          
          
        
      351. 
      
        
    351. 
          1
          
              def total_pages
        
      352.

              # Recursively merge into target hash by using stringified keys from the other one
        
      360. 
      
        
    360. 
          1
          
              def stringified_merge(target, other)
        
      361. 
      
        
    361. 
          
          
                other.each do |key, value|
        
      362. 
      
        
    362. 
          
          
                  key = key.to_s # this line is what it's all about!
        
      363. 
      
        
    363. 
          
          
                  existing = target[key]
        
      364. 
      
        
    364. 
          
          
          
        
      365. 
      
        
    365. 
          
          
                  if value.is_a?(Hash) and (existing.is_a?(Hash) or existing.nil?)
        
      366. 
      
        
    366. 
          
          
                    stringified_merge(existing || (target[key] = {}), value)
        
      367. 
      
        
    367. 
          
          
                  else
        
      368. 
      
        
    368. 
          
          
                    target[key] = value
        
      369. 
      
        
    369. 
          
          
                  end
        
      370. 
      
        
    370. 
          
          
                end
        
      371. 
      
        
    371. 
          
          
              end
        
      372. 
      
        
    372. 
          
          
            end
        
      373. 
      
        
    373. 
          
          
          end
